beginSubroutine: s32'Init_Boss'
  cpuGuardLevelBonus: 0, 80
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddAttackRate), Val(10)
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(75)
  callSubroutine: s32'SkillSet'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Init_EX_Boss'
  cpuGuardLevelBonus: 0, 100
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddAttackRate), Val(10)
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(125)
  callSubroutine: s32'SkillSet'
  if: Mem(EXBoss)
    callSubroutine: s32'EX_SkillSet'
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

postSubroutineBegin: s32'CPUEstimate'
  callSubroutine: s32'Boss_Estimate'
  if: Mem(EXBoss)
    callSubroutine: s32'EX_Estimate'
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Boss_Estimate'
  ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
      skillHighEstimation: s32'Chain1'
      skillHighEstimation: s32'Chain2'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
      skillHighEstimation: s32'Chain3'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'EX_Estimate'
  ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tension), Val(5000)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(550000)
        skillHighEstimation: s32'unblockable1'
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(800000)
          skillHighEstimation: s32'unblockable2'
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  checkLastAttackHitStateName: 22, s32'ELP_Ultimate2_exe'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    skillHighEstimation: s32'Bombo1'
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(13)
      debugLogForScript: s32'93', 0, 0
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(1)
      findState: s32'cmn_AfroObj', 11, 2, 52
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 940
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(14)
      debugLogForScript: s32'97', 0, 0
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 540
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(15)
      debugLogForScript: s32'273', 0, 0
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          debugLogForScript: s32'afro', 0, 3
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 1000
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(12)
      debugLogForScript: s32'337', 0, 0
      displayMesh: s32'Head_high', 0
      displayMesh: s32'Headhighfau', 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  endIf: 
endSubroutine:
